shared_focus = {
	id = ita_let_sleeping_sailors_sleep
	icon = GFX_focus_generic_navy_talk
	cost = 4.00
	prerequisite = {
		focus = ita_a_defensive_mindset_is_necessary
	}

	mutually_exclusive = {
		focus = ita_end_the_navy_primacy
	}

	x = 27
	y = 7
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ita_let_sleeping_sailors_sleep"
		add_stability = 0.02
		add_to_variable = {
			var = ITA_Sogno_RoyalNavy
			value = 2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { ITA_Sogno_RoyalNavy > 5 }
			}
			set_variable = { ITA_Sogno_RoyalNavy = 5 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { ITA_Sogno_RoyalNavy < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { ITA_Sogno_RoyalNavy = 0 }
		}

		add_to_variable = {
			var = ITA_Sogno_Carabinieri
			value = -2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { ITA_Sogno_Carabinieri > 5 }
			}
			set_variable = { ITA_Sogno_Carabinieri= 5 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { ITA_Sogno_Carabinieri < 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { ITA_Sogno_Carabinieri = 0 }
		}
	}
}

			set_variable = { ITA_Sogno_RoyalNavy = 0 }
		}

			value = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { ITA_Sogno_RoyalArmy > 5 }
			}
			set_variable = { ITA_Sogno_RoyalArmy = 5 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { ITA_Sogno_RoyalArmy < 0 } }
			set_variable = { ITA_Sogno_RoyalArmy = 0 }
		}

		add_to_variable = {
			var = ITA_Sogno_RoyalAirforce
			value = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { ITA_Sogno_RoyalAirforce > 5 }

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = socialist
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = socialist
				popularity = 0.02
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = progressivism
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = progressivism
				popularity = 0.02
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = liberalism
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = liberalism
				popularity = 0.02
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = -0.01
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternalism
			popularity = -0.01
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communist
			popularity = -0.01
		}
		TNO_improve_poverty_med = yes
	}
}

shared_focus = {
	id = ita_strategia_del_cambio
	icon = GFX_focus_generic_change_law_speech
	cost = 2.00
	x = 12
	y = 2
	prerequisite = {
		focus = ita_devalue_the_lira
	}
	prerequisite = {
		focus = ita_revamp_the_export_infrastructure
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ita_strategia_del_cambio"
		USA = {
			set_variable = { TEMPINTEREST = interest_rates }
		}
		ITA = {
			set_temp_variable = { x_VAR_INTER = TEMPINTEREST }
			set_temp_variable = { neg_x_VAR_INTER = interest_rates }
			multiply_temp_variable = { neg_x_VAR_INTER = -1 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { x_VAR_INTER = neg_x_VAR_INTER }
			add_to_temp_variable = { x_VAR_INTER = TEMPINTEREST }
			add_to_temp_variable = { x_VAR_INTER = .01 }
			set_variable = { interest_rates = x_VAR_INTER }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ita_strategia_del_cambio_tt
	}
}
